<Rating>1<//Rating>< Text>
For my husband and my wedding in December of 2017, we decided to get married closest to my family in Southern California. Our reception was outside, and since it gets cold after sunset, we decided to rent two large outdoor propane space heaters, and two 3' tall pillars for decoration from this business.
The pillars worked fine, because they just stood where we placed them, the heaters, however, did not work at all.
My father-in-law, half of the groomsmen, and a couple guests worked for the majority of the reception trying to get the heaters to work. We called the rental company for assistance, and they said, "Sorry, that's your problem."
We followed the instructions to the "T" to start them, and even researched troubleshooting procedures online--still to no avail. They could not get the propane to flow.

Throughout the reception, we heard our guests complaining about the cold, and most left, which is the last thing a new bride wants to at her own wedding reception.

The following morning, my in-laws took the the heaters back to the rental company, and explained everything that transpired. The faculty at "All occasions Party Rentals" tried to start them and couldn't either. The staff told them, "It's not our problem either" and took the heaters back without reimbursing my Family at all.
We would have not paid if they had not required us to pay in advance as a non-refundable deposit of nearly  $300 dollars.
My father-in-law believes they overfilled the propane tanks which set an internal safety valve from allowing any propane to flow.

These folks gave us terrible customer service, and terrible equipment. They cost us a good sum of money for nonoperational heaters, and ruined our reception.

I greatly recommend you steer clear of these people if you are looking for equipment to depend on, and good customer service.</Text>

<Review>First and foremost, I want to preface this review by saying that prior to being a member of Fitness 19, I was at 24 Hour Fitness for 15 years.

While 24 Hour Fitness was an ideal gym for me, COVID hit, and life happened. I am up 45/50 lbs and for someone who was into powerlifting and squatted a PR of 455, being fat and weak is no bueno for me. I was, I‚Äôm sure, one of many people who chose not to go to gym due to the possibility of suffering the consequences of catching this life-threatening virus and bringing it home to our loved ones who are or aren‚Äôt health compromised but the bottom line is, yes- I did not make good choices when it came to my health.

However, I made the decision to cancel my 24 Hour Fitness membership last year as they were no longer 24 hours open and reservations were to be made for 1-hour workouts. I then signed up online for the $30 membership at Fitness 19 and was very impressed with how avid the young men in the front would clean and mist the machines while enforcing the mask rule. I understand that many do not agree with wearing masks at the gym but for the safety of all myself and gym members, i greatly appreciated it.

I have gone to the Yorba Linda Fitness 19 as My office is there and have to comment about how disrespectful and thoughtless the members and staff are at that location. Cleaning machines prior/after use is something rarely seen from the members there. And masks? HA! You would think that covid doesn‚Äôt exist in that part of town. The young man at the front desk is always on his phone and does not clean any machines.

So, after a long hiatus, I returned to Fitness 19 Brea and was greeted by Miss Coco who I have to say is truly the sweetest woman. I look forward to my early morning workouts knowing that a staff member like herself cares about the well-being of all gym members. The members at this gym are far more respectful and courteous than the YL gym.

So there is no doubt when choosing a gym - sign up at Fitness 19.<//Review></record>

< Text>
One of my favorite wineries for wine tasting. Price of tasting is very affordable ($15) and is waived if you buy a bottle of wine, which are also priced well - in $20-$30 range. The best part is that they encourage you to walk around, sit outside, etcetera and they come find you with the next wine in the tasting list. While technically speaking you can do this anywhere, this is the first place I didn't feel like I had to ask. They also have chickens walking around which are adorable, and colorful chairs under a tree facing the vineyard which makes for the most relaxing place to sit and sip.</Text>

< review>
Ahhh-mazing! I had to take my 11 1/2 month old son in to be seen. He started walking early and chipped one of his lower teeth. :( As soon as we walked in, he wasn't clinging to me like most new places. He saw toys and magazines to play with. New patient paperwork was electronic on an iPad. The area for seeing the hygienist is friendly and open. TVs at each station for distraction. We got to watch our favorite YouTube channel which made him excited enough stand on the table and babble. I was incorporated into the visit to help hold my son so he felt more at ease. We learned how to brush teeth properly. Dr. Evans saw him and was super friendly. My son gave him a high five! He cried to have fluoride on his teeth and to get his tooth filed smooth but only because he had to be horizontal which is currently not his favorite (doesn't want to lay down for diapers right now). There was no sedation needed. Dr. Evans did the filing less than 2 minutes and then my baby was back to normal. We got our name on the cavity free wall AND a token for a prize (ball) which he loved. When we left he waved goodbye with ball in hand! Hands down the best experience for children! Would recommend to my friends and family.< /review>

< Review>
Went to iDessert while on vacation in San Diego. Located in the Little Italy neighborhood, this spot is just a stones-throw away from numerous amazing places to eat. Once you're done with your dinner, definitely save time and room for this place.

This place let's you build your dessert from the ground up. Choosing the different flavors of the cake, cream, and the meringue shell. Top it all off with the Vegas Bowl add-on. It doesn't add anything to the taste of the dessert, but it sure does look cool.< /Review>

<rate>3< /rate>< Text>
Desserts are overpriced, but nice to photograph for Instagram. You order on an iPad and can choose how you want your meringue to be made. Simple options for cake, sauce, fruit, filling. Nice place to visit once, but there are better dessert spots to visit. There's also an option to have your dessert served in a bowl with nitrogen for $1.50 more...Waste of money. It looks cool for about 5 seconds, but in the process it melts your ice cream and turns the plastic bowls hot. Caution around kids is recommended if you opt for the Las Vegas meringue bowl.</Text>

< text>
I highly recommend this place! The concept was great! The staff was very friendly and the place looks so chic and very pleasing to the eyes! Boyfriend chose this place when we were looking for a dessert place. I didn‚Äôt know what this place is or what it was offering, until we arrive! And my gosh! As soon as we walked in, I feel in love with the place! ‚ù§Ô∏è

There was not a lot of people when we went here as it was raining. There were actually only two couples inside. We went to the front because my boyfriend and I were clueless on how everything works, the staff at the register explained everything well. We chose to customize our own dessert so we went to one of the iPads on the wall. We chose meringue because this is what they are really known for! They offer a lot more kind of desserts like cakes, shakes, etc.! But my boyfriend and I wanted to try the meringue. They have 16 different meringues, all were handcrafted and looks so pretty! The customization process on the iPad was so easy to go through, it was user friendly. You can always go back to the previous step if you want to change something on your order before submitting it! After submitting our order and paying it on the iPad, the staff at the front had immediately started making our customized meringue!

The wait time for our meringue was not that bad, I think we waited for like 6-7 minutes before we were called. When we finally got our order, my boyfriend and I were both excited for it! The taste was heavenly! It was so good! We both enjoyed it so much! The dessert is not only pretty, it was also delicious!</text>

< userid>
106311527544042101385</userid>
<username>Lorie Lacasa< /username><time>1479506282718< /time><Rate>5</Rate>< Text>
I found out about this place just walking through little italy. I remember being drawn in by their interior design and unusually placed ipads at the counter. There was a case on the wall that was filled with these round things (crust), so I wanted to see what it was all about.

I built my own dessert. It's an innovative dessert concept- you pick a crust (16+ to choose from), and pick a gelato/sorbet to go in it. You also get to pick a cake (5 flavors), and a cream, sauce or fruit to go with it. If you want to be extra fancy, you can get the vegas bowl to have that dry ice effect in the photos.

I went with a coffee crust, mocha gelato, spiced vanilla cream, vanilla cake and some caramel sauce. Clearly I was going for a coffee/chai kind of dessert, but I loved it! The vegas bowl adds to the coolness factor - it's just so out of this world. It's definitely a game changer in the san diego area, and the possibilities are endless!

Writing this review just makes me want to go back - it is pretty pricey though. Depending on all your add-ons, you can easily spend $10.<//Text>

< date>
1464292894531<//date>
<Rating>3</Rating>< text>
iDessert is a fancy made-to-order gelato dessert place created by famous chef Jean-Philippe.

You create your dessert with an ipad. You get to choose your meringue shell, gelato flavor, whether you want cake, fruit, and cream flavor. If you're feeling extra fancy and plan on instagramming your dessert, pay extra for the dry ice so you get that cool effect of a fog.

It looks cool, but I thought the dessert was okay. I wasn't a fan of the meringue shell. The gelato melted too fast. The dessert as a whole wasn't anything mindblowing. For me, it is a one time experience kind of place.

Place is small. They dont have enough tables. It sucks if the place is packed because this isn't the type of dessert that you can grab and eat while walking.<//text>
